    <script>
(function (doc) {
    "use strict";
    if (device.type === "mobile") {
        var creatFocusList = function () {
                var box = doc.getElementById("js_focus_box");
                var htmls = ['<div class="piccont" id="js_focus"><div id="js_focus_in">'];
                htmls.push(creatOneList(focusData[focusData.length - 1]));
                for(var i = 0, iLen = focusData.length; i < iLen; i++) {
                    htmls.push(creatOneList(focusData[i]));
                }
                htmls.push(creatOneList(focusData[0]));
                htmls.push('</div></div><div class="fucusbar"><a class="prev" href="javascript:void(0);"></a><a class="next" href="javascript:void(0);"></a></div>');
                box.innerHTML = htmls.join("");

        };
        var creatOneList = function (data) {
            return '<div class="pic"><a href="' + data.url + '" title="' + data.title + '" ><img src="' + data.image + '" alt="' + data.title + '" /></a><span class="shadow"><a href="' + data.url + '" title="' + data.title + '">' + data.title + '</a></span></div>';
        }
        creatFocusList();
    } else {
            var fcDomId = 'js_focus_box';

            var $id = function (id) {
                return document.getElementById(id);
            };

            var fcDom = $id(fcDomId);
            
            if (fcDom !== null && typeof focusData !== 'undefined') {
                //整体模板
              var whole = function () {
                var arr = [];
                arr.push('<div class="focus">');
                //文字列表焦点背景图  
                arr.push( '<div id="js_wfocus_bg" class="focalize" style="top:0px;">');
                arr.push(   '<span></span>');
                arr.push( '</div>');
                  
                arr.push( '<span class="focus_shadow"></span>');
                //文字列表  
                arr.push( '<ul id="js_words_list"></ul>');      
                  
                arr.push( '<div class="picture" style="left:120px;">');
                //图片列表
                arr.push(   '<div id="js_imgs_list" class="picture_main"></div>');
                
                arr.push( '</div>');
                arr.push('</div>');

                return arr.join('');
              };

              //文字列表模板
              var wordsList = function (dataList) {
                var arr = [];
                var className = '';                
                for (var i = 0, l = dataList.length; i < l; i++) {
                    className = (i === 0) ? 'current' : '';
                    var data = dataList[i];
                  arr.push('<li class="' + className + '" data-num="' + i + '">');
                  arr.push(  '<a href="' + data.url + '" target="video">');
                  arr.push(    '<em>' + data.title + '</em>');
                  arr.push(  '</a>');
                  arr.push('</li>');
                }
                
                return arr.join('');
              };

              //图片列表模板
              var imgsList = function (dataList) {
                var arr = [];
                for (var i = 0, l = dataList.length; i < l; i++) {
                    var data = dataList[i];
                    arr.push('<div class="picture_box">');
                  arr.push(    '<a href="' + data.url + '" target="video">');
                  arr.push(        '<img src="' + data.image + '" alt="" title="' + data.title + '">');
                  arr.push(    '</a>');
                  arr.push('</div>');
                }

                return arr.join('');
              };      

              //内容生成
              fcDom.innerHTML = whole();

              var wordsListDom = $id('js_words_list'),
                    imgsListDom = $id('js_imgs_list');
              //拼装数据
              wordsListDom.innerHTML = wordsList(focusData);
              imgsListDom.innerHTML = imgsList(focusData);
            }
    }
}(document));

			var domain = document.domain.substr(0, (document.domain.length - 10)); //处理域名
			var href = document.location.href;
			var start = href.lastIndexOf("/") + 1;
			var end = href.lastIndexOf(".");
			href = href.substr(start, end - start); //获取页面的唯一值
			var cookie_time = new Date();
			var ti = cookie_time.getFullYear().toString() + (cookie_time.getMonth() + 1).toString() + cookie_time.getDate().toString(); //获取日期
			var url_start = url.indexOf("-") + 1;
			url = url.substr(url_start, 20);
			var url_end = url.indexOf("-");
			url = url.substr(0, url_end);
			flag_cookie = domain + url + href + ti;
			return flag_cookie;
		},

div_height:400,	 // 页面内容的宽度
div_step_px:30,	 // 页面每次下推或上拉的尺寸	如 5
div_step_time:100,	 // 页面每隔多长时间进行一次下推或上拉操作，单位：毫秒	 如 100
div_timeout:5,	 // 页面展开后，过多长时间进行回缩，单位：毫秒
div_speed:0.1,

img:null,	 //	JS	动态创建的 img
time_interval_down:null,	//	向上推事件变量
time_interval_up:null,	 //	向上回缩事件变量
time_out:null,	 //	超时
div:null,	 //	JS	动态创建的 div
div_a:null,	 //	JS	动态创建的 a

play:function() {
var Fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();

this.div = document.createElement('div');
this.div.id = 'ifenngFullScreen_div';
this.div.style.width = this.div_width + 'px';
this.div.style.height = this.div_height + 'px';
this.div.style.border = '0px';
this.div.style.marginLeft = 'auto';
this.div.style.marginRight = 'auto';

this.div_a.target = '_blank';

this.div.appendChild(this.div_a);
Fragment.appendChild(this.div);

document.body.insertBefore(Fragment, document.body.firstChild);
},
control_down:function(){
var div = document.getElementById('ifenngFullScreen_div');
if(div == null) return;
var marginTop = div.style.marginTop;
marginTop = marginTop.replace('px', '');
//div_step_px = div_step_px * (div_speed + 1);
marginTop = parseInt(marginTop) + IFENGFULLSCREEN.div_step_px;
div.style.marginTop = marginTop + "px";
if(parseInt(marginTop) >= parseInt(0)) {
div.style.marginTop = "0px";
//div_step_px = 1;
window.clearInterval(IFENGFULLSCREEN.time_interval_down);
IFENGFULLSCREEN.time_out = setTimeout(IFENGFULLSCREEN.control_time_up, IFENGFULLSCREEN.div_timeout*1000);
}
},
control_up:function() {
var marginTop = IFENGFULLSCREEN.div.style.marginTop;
marginTop = marginTop.replace('px', '');
marginTop = parseInt(marginTop) - IFENGFULLSCREEN.div_step_px;
IFENGFULLSCREEN.div.style.marginTop = marginTop + "px";
if(parseInt(marginTop) < parseInt('-' + IFENGFULLSCREEN.div_height)) {
IFENGFULLSCREEN.div.style.marginTop = '-'+ IFENGFULLSCREEN.div_height +'px';
//document.body.removeChild(IFENGFULLSCREEN.div);
window.clearInterval(IFENGFULLSCREEN.time_interval_up);
}
},
control_time_up:function() {
IFENGFULLSCREEN.time_interval_up = window.setInterval(IFENGFULLSCREEN.control_up, parseInt(IFENGFULLSCREEN.div_step_time));
},

init:function(url_img,url_a,div_width,div_height,div_step_px,div_step_time,div_timeout,div_speed) {

this.div_height = div_height;
}

//得到一个cookie的值
 function getcookie(name) {
	var splitCookie = document.cookie.split("; ");
	for(var i = 0; i < splitCookie.length; i++) {
		var cookieNameValue = splitCookie[i].split("=");
		if(cookieNameValue[0] == name) {
			return unescape(cookieNameValue[1]);
		}
	}
	return '';
}
//种一个cookie
 function setcookie(name, value, time) {
	var date = new Date();
	var expiresTime = new Date(date.getTime() + time * 1000);
	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) + ";path=/;expires=" + expiresTime.toGMTString() + ";";
}
this.img.onload = function() {	
				var url = document.location.href;
				var cookiename = "autoFullScreen" + escape(url.substr(url.indexOf('/', 7), 2) + url.substring(url.lastIndexOf('/'))) ;
				var cookieId = getcookie(cookiename);
				//判断当前应该播放哪一个广告
				if(cookieId == ''){
				//播放广告
					IFENGFULLSCREEN.play();
					setcookie(cookiename,1,86400);
				}	
}
}
};

var ifengFullScreen_div_width = 1000;	 // 页面内容的宽度

var fullScreenNowHours = fullScreenNowDate.getHours();
if(typeof fullScreenList != 'undefined'){
		for(var i = 0; i < fullScreenList.length; i++){
			fullScreenStartTime = fullScreenList[i][2];
			fullScreenEndTime = fullScreenList[i][3];
			if(typeof fullScreenStartTime != 'undefined' && typeof fullScreenEndTime != 'undefined' && fullScreenNowHours >= fullScreenStartTime && fullScreenNowHours < fullScreenEndTime){
				ifengFullScreen_url_img = fullScreenList[i][0];
				ifengFullScreen_url_a = fullScreenList[i][1];
				IFENGFULLSCREEN.init(ifengFullScreen_url_img,ifengFullScreen_url_a,ifengFullScreen_div_width);
			}
		}
	}

		var maxTimes = obj.maxTimes;
		var adContent = '';
		var elements = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('code');
		var fixtures = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('cite');
		//轮播控制cookie
		var cookieFlag = 'ifengRotator_'+ identifier;
		var current = _.getcookie(cookieFlag);
		var timeOut = 43200;//过期时间
		var element,tempStr;
		if(typeof current === 'undefined' || current == ''){
			current =  parseInt(Math.random() * 100000) % maxTimes;
		}
		//频次控制cookie
		var ifengWindowCookieName = 'ifengWindowCookieName' + _.getSecondDomain();
		if(_.getcookie(ifengWindowCookieName)!=1){
			_.setcookie(cookieFlag, ((parseInt(current) + 1) % maxTimes), timeOut);
			if(typeof elements[current] != 'undefined'){
			element = elements[current];
			adContent = element.innerHTML;
		}
		if(adContent == ''){
			if(typeof fixtures[0] != 'undefined'){
				element = fixtures[0];
				adContent = element.innerHTML;
			}
		}
		adContent = adContent.replace('<!--BOF', '');
		adContent = adContent.replace('EOF-->', '');
		}
		//频次控制
		var date=new Date();
		if(_.getcookie(ifengWindowCookieName)!=1){
			showIfengWindow();
		}
		function showIfengWindow(){
			document.write(adContent);
			_.setcookie(ifengWindowCookieName, 1, obj.showIntervalTime);	
		}
	};
	ifengWindow.prototype = {
		//得到一个cookie的值
		getcookie : function(name) {
			var splitCookie = document.cookie.split("; ");
			for(var i = 0; i < splitCookie.length; i++) {
				var cookieNameValue = splitCookie[i].split("=");
				if(cookieNameValue[0] == name) {
					return unescape(cookieNameValue[1]);
				}
			}
			return '';
		},
		//种一个cookie
		setcookie : function(name, value, time) {
			var date = new Date();
			var expiresTime = new Date(date.getTime() + time * 1000);
			document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) + ";path=/;expires=" + expiresTime.toGMTString() + ";";
		},
		//获得二级域名（频道域名）
		getSecondDomain : function() {
				var arr_domain=document.domain.split(".");
				return arr_domain[0];
		}
	}
	new ifengWindow({
		showIntervalTime : 600,  //视窗showIntervalTime秒内展示一次
		maxTimes : 1, //广告流量
		identifier : 'Ap2623'
	});
</script>
<!--/s_itv_index_ad_media-->
